***иллюстрировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иллюстрировать.html>иллюстри́ровать</a> (14618)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">illustrieren</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иллюстрировать.html>иллюстри́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">illjustrírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr> or <abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:иллюстрировать.html>иллюстри́ровать</a></strong></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проиллюстри́ровать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to illustrate</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иллюстрация.html>иллюстра́ция</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">illjustrácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">иллюстрати́вный</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">illjustratívnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:именитый.html>имени́тый</a> (17434)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">имен-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imen-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́тый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:именитый.html>имени́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">imenítyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>distinguished, eminent</li></ol>

***именно.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>именно</a> (210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:именной.html>именно́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imennój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>и́менно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ímenno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>just, exactly, actually; used to emphasize the meaning of the following word or what comes later and sometimes can be rather difficult to translate it in English.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>ра́з</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kak ráz</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собственный.html>со́бственно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sóbstvenno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:произойти.html>произошло́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>именно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:предполагать.html>предполага́л</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vsjó proizošlo <b>imenno</b> tak kak ja predpolagal.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Everything happened just as I'd supposed.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кто.html>Кто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>зна́ет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>именно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живёт</a>...</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Kto jevo znajet gde <b>imenno</b> on živjót...</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Who knows where exactly he lives...</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:статья.html>Статья́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:появиться.html>появи́лась</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:газета.html>газе́те</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>именно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницу</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Statʹja pojavilasʹ v gazete <b>imenno</b> v pjatnicu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The article appeared in the newspaper just on Friday.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>Именно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассказать.html>рассказа́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:правда.html>пра́вду</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Imenno</b> on mne rasskazal vsju pravdu.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Actually he was the one who told me all the truth.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">usually as "<a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>именно</a>"</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> namely, to wit, rather; used to specify something or when listing to specify something.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:частность.html>ча́стности</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">v částnosti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бишь.html>бишь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tó bišʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:собственный.html>со́бственно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sóbstvenno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>го́ду</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сезон.html>сезо́на</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>именно</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:весна.html>весна́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:осень.html>о́сень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:зима.html>зима́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V godu četyre sezona, a <b>imenno</b> — vesna, leto, osenʹ i zima.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">There are four seasons in a year, namely the spring, the summer, the autumn, and the winter.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>тот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>именно</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́ту</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:произойти.html>произошло́</a> ЧП.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V tot denʹ, a <b>imenno</b> v subbotu, proizošlo ČP.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That day, or rather on Saturday, there was an emergency.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>Она</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>живёт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> Нью-Йорке, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>именно</a></b> — <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> Уолл-стрит.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ona živjót v Nʹju-Jorke, a <b>imenno</b> — na Uoll-strit.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">She lives in New York, to wit, on the Wall Street.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>и́менно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ímenno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>indeed, rather; used to emphasize the agreement or confirmation.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:естественно.html>есте́ственно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jestéstvenno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:конечно.html>коне́чно</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">konéčno</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">"<a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́те</a>?" "<b><a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>Именно</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вам</a>!"</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">"Vy mne eto govorite?" "<b>Imenno</b>, Vam!"</i> ― <span class="e-translation">"Are you telling me such things?" "You, indeed!"</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">"<a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>Ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хо́чешь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чтоб.html>чтоб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>тебе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассказать.html>рассказа́ла</a>?" "<b><a href = vnd.unilang:именно.html>Именно</a></b>!"</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">"Ty xočešʹ štob ja tebe vsjó rasskazala?" "<b>Imenno</b>!"</i> ― <span class="e-translation">"Do you want me to tell you everything?" "Rather!"</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***иметь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a> (123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*jьměti</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">мець</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjecʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">ма́ти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">máty</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">mieć</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">имати</i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">imati</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">имѣти</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iměti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">imétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to have, to possess
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хочу́</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a></strong> <a href = vnd.unilang:друг.html>друзе́й</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja xočú imétʹ druzéj.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I want to have friends.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>Име́ть</a> is rarely used in Russian, except with non-physical objects and most often in set expressions ("To have in mind," or "To have rights,"). The most common way to express normal possession is "<a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> + genitive possessor + <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a> + nominative possession."
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:иметься.html>име́ться</a> (1144)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметься.html>име́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">imétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be, to be present, to be available, to there is / there are
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>на́шем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́роде</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:иметься.html>име́ется</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:театр.html>теа́тра</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V nášem górode <b>iméjetsja</b> dva teátra.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>There are</b> two theatres in our town/city.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:иметься.html>име́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>виду́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совсем.html>совсе́м</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:другой.html>друго́е</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Imélosʹ</b> v vidú sovsém drugóje.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Something quite different <b>was</b> meant (from "<a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>виду</a>" - to mean, to have in mind).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***имеющий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:имеющий.html>име́ющий</a> (123)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***имитировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:имитировать.html>имити́ровать</a> (16715)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">imitieren</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:имитировать.html>имити́ровать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">imitírovatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сымити́ровать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mimic, to imitate
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:имитировать.html>имити́ровать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>голоса</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:животный.html>живо́тных</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>imitírovatʹ</b> golosa živótnyx</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to mimic the voices of animals</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to simulate</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">imitate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:подражать.html>подража́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">podražátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изображать.html>изобража́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izobražátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">подде́лывать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">poddélyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сымити́ровать</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">symitírovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иммиграция.html>иммигра́ция</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">immigrácija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́нный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ónnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***император.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:император.html>импера́тор</a> (2272)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">imperātor</i>. The feminine form is influenced by the oblique stem (compare the ablative singular <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">imperātrīce</i>) of Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">imperātrīx</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_4">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:императрица.html>императри́ца</a> (14122)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Originally borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">imperātrīx</i> via its oblique stem (compare the ablative singular <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">imperātrīce</i>), but the resulting form may also be interpreted as an in-house Russian Slavic derivation from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:император.html>импера́тор</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">imperator</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> with the suffix <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ица</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***империалист.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:империалист.html>империали́ст</a> (20953)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:империалист.html>империали́ст</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">imperialíst</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:империалист.html>империали́ста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:империалист.html>империали́сты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:империалист.html>империали́стов</a></b>)
